Prepare to see the results of the top famous person:\n- Define a predicate \"see_results\" that takes in a list of objects and returns a list of objects.\n- Use recursion to iterate through the list and check if each object is a famous person.\n- If a famous person is found, use the \"view_results\" predicate to see their results.\n- Return the updated list of objects.\n\n10. Prepare to be equalitarian-minded:\n- Define a predicate \"be_equalitarian\" that takes in a list of objects and returns a list of objects.\n- Use recursion to iterate through the list and check if each object is a social-minded person.\n- If a social-minded person is found, use the \"become_equalitarian\" predicate to become equalitarian-minded.\n- Return the updated list of objects."]]
